and to take appropriate action to correct the infraction including the issuance of a warning violation notice or removal from the course for the remainder of that day remainder of that season one calendar year or in only the most egregious instances permanent banishment when taking action the course official shall take into consideration the seriousness of the violation the number of violations on that day the number of past violations and the harm caused by the violation action under this section may be in place of or in addition to referral of the matter to the roosevelt police department for enforcement of criminal penalties any person subject to a warning violation notice or removal for any period of time under this section may appeal the decision all initial appeals shall be heard by the golf professional unless the golf professional was the person who first found there to be a violation if the violation was first addressed by the golf professional then the city manager shall hear the initial appeal in the golf professionals place all appeals must be filed in writing within fourteen 14 days of the action taken against the individual appeals shall be considered filed when delivered to the roosevelt city office on a day it is open for business and during regular business hours the fourteen 14 day time limitation shall extend to the close of business on the first business day for which the city offices are open for business after the fourteenth day following the violation the city manager shall ensure that a hearing date is set and that the appealing party is notified of said date within ten 10 days of receiving the written appeal the appealing party may be present to address the golf professional at the scheduled meeting if they so choose the golf professional will consider the matter regardless of whether the appealing party chooses to be present the golf professional shall take into consideration the written appeal any information provided in person by the appealing party and any information provided by the course official who took action against the appealing party the golf professional may either affirm or suspend the action taken against the appealing party any person whose appeal has been heard by the golf professional or city manager when applicable may appeal the decision of the golf professional to the roosevelt city council all appeals must be filed in writing within fourteen 14 days of the golf professionals decision appeals shall be considered filed when delivered to the roosevelt city office on a day it is open for business and during regular business hours the fourteen 14 day time limitation shall extend to the close of business on the first business day for which the city offices are open for business after the fourteenth day following the violation the city manager shall ensure that the appealing party is notified of the date of the next regularly scheduled city council meeting within ten 10 days of receiving the written appeal the appealing party may be present to address the city council at their regularly scheduled meeting if they so choose the city council will consider the matter regardless of whether the appealing party chooses to be present at its first regularly scheduled meeting following the date the appealing party is notified of the meeting date the city council shall take into consideration the written appeal any information provided in person by the appealing party and any information provided by the course official who took action against the appealing party the city council may either affirm or suspend the action taken against the appealing party   part part1 prior legislation parks definitions use of parks users fee for park pavilions  definitions of burial rights ownership responsibilities  definitions the following words or phrases shall have the following meanings unless the context otherwise clearly requires lot means and includes the partial lots or single graves in the municipal cemetery lot owner or purchaser and grave owner or purchaser mean the owner or purchaser of burial privileges or the collateral right of use of any burial lot evidenced by a deed or burial right for a described lot or by proved and recognized descent or devise from the original owner   name of burial ground the burial ground of this municipality shall be known and designated by the name of roosevelt memorial park   cemeteries covered by chapter all cemeteries owned andor maintained by the municipality or which may hereafter be acquired by the municipality wherever situated are declared subject to the provisions of this chapter   office of cemetery superintendent there is created the position of cemetery superintendent   duties of cemetery superintendent the cemetery superintendent subject to direction by the city council city administrator and parks and recreation director shall be responsible for the cemetery and is authorized to enforce the rules and regulations of the city code pertaining to the cemetery he shall take such action as may be necessary as authorized by the code to protect the property grave sites and cemetery in general from injury or loss and to preserve the peace and good order in the cemetery and shall have the general supervision and administration of the cemetery including but not limited to arecommending to the governing body such additional rules and regulations as may be necessary for the operation maintenance use and protection of the cemetery  bsubdividing the cemetery into lots and grave sites  cmaintaining a record of the location of the graves and preventing any lot from being used beyond its capacity  dkeeping in proper repair the enclosure around the cemetery and preventing its being entered by animals and so far as practical preventing the destruction or defacing of any tablet or marker placed or erected therein  ekeeping a duplicate plat of the cemetery and at the request of any person wishing to purchase any of the lots or parts of lots pointing out any of the lots or parts of lots for sale  and upon disposal of any lots or part thereof notifying the recorderclerk of such fact the recorderclerk shall after payment of the lot price has been received in the treasury issue a certificate of burial rights which shall describe the lot or grave to which the right to burial is granted the certificate shall be signed by the mayor and the recorderclerk  fopening any graves in the cemetery upon application to him being made by the recorderclerk or by any person having the right to make such application and being responsible for closing all graves  gremoving floral pieces or displays left on any grave as deemed necessary to the appearance of the cemetery but such floral pieces or displays shall not be removed sooner than seven days after original placement except in emergency  hkeeping the streets alleys walks and avenues in the cemetery in good order and unobstructed  ierecting a suitable marker firmly set upon the northwest corner of each lot with the number of the lot inscribed thereon and which location shall be shown on the cemetery records part  prior code  8212  burials aburial sitesdefinitionsrules 1general burial site is construed to mean a space eight feet by four feet 2baby grave site is construed to mean a space four feet by four feet two baby graves may be buried on a single general burial site provided authorization is granted by the purchasers if still living or designated person having the original right of burial if purchasers is are deceased 3urn grave site allows no more than two urns be buried on one general grave site 4combined grave sites generally no more than one burial per grave site will be allowed in a general burial site except for atwo urns btwo babies cone urnbaby done regular burialone urn bdelivery for burial the deceased must be delivered to the cemetery at or before twothirty pm for interment so the grave can be filled with earth that same day there will be an overtime charge for burials requiring work after regular working hours cprohibited burial days burials shall not occur on christmas new years day memorial day saturday before memorial day fourth of july labor day thanksgiving day and sundays this includes one day prior to the holiday and one day after dbefore any deceased person is buried in the municipal cemetery a permit properly issued by the registrar of the registration district in which the death occurred or in the absence of such registrar a permit duly issued by the state division of health or other authorized person shall be required by the cemetery sexton after burial the cemetery sexton shall endorse upon the permit a description of the location where the deceased is buried and shall enter all information contained in the permit in the cemetery records part prior code  8221  burial permit it is unlawful for any person to bury the body of a deceased person in the municipal cemetery without first obtaining a certificate of burial right for the lot used or producing satisfactory evidence of a right to burial based on a properly acquired certificate of burial right   registration of burials before any deceased person may be buried in the municipal cemetery the relatives or person having charge of the deceased shall provide the recorderclerk with a written statement which shall be filed by the recorderclerk which statement shall contain if known information about the deceased regarding his or her name when and where born the date and cause of death the name of the attending physician date of burial name of cemetery and the description of the location of the grave   burials and disinterment ait is an infraction for any person to 1disinter any body buried in any cemetery except under the direction of the cemetery superintendent who shall before disinterment require written permission from both the municipal health officer and the owner of the lot or his or her heirs which written authorization shall be filed and preserved in a record kept for such purposes  2disinter or remove the body of a person who has died from a contagious disease within two years after the date of burial unless the body was buried in a hermetically sealed casket or vault and is found to be so incased at the time of disinterment bit is an infraction to inter anything other than the remains of human bodies in cemeteries cit is an infraction to bury the body of any person within this municipality except in the municipal cemetery or a private cemetery unless by special permission of the governing body under such rules and regulations that it may prescribe ddisinterments will be made by the cemetery superintendent only upon receiving a court order and advance payment of the fee for disinterments as set by the city council the fee is set by resolution of the city council and is subject to change without notice part  prior code  8224  vaults required aunless in writing waived by the cemetery superintendent it is unlawful for any person to be buried in the cemetery unless the casket shall be placed in a vault made of concrete fiberglass steel or bricklined or of such other material approved by the governing body substantially constructed and covered with a similar durable material bno wood shall be used as a permanent part of the construction of any part of the vault   religious and fraternal organizations the municipality may contract with religious and fraternal organizations to designate a reasonable portion of the cemetery in which burials may be restricted to members of such religious and fraternal organizations and their families   sale subject to rules every lot or single grave sold is subject to rules and regulations that have been or may be adopted the rules and regulations shall be subject to such changes as are found necessary for the protection of lot owners the remains of the dead and the preservation of the cemetery   care reserved the municipality reserves the right to enter upon any grave and to perform all work necessary for the care and upkeep of all lots and graves in its cemeteries   orders and responsibilities for errors under no circumstances will the municipality assume responsibilities for errors in opening graves when orders are given by telephone   traffic rules athe provisions of the municipal traffic ordinances relative to the operation of vehicles and conduct of pedestrians shall be in effect in the cemetery except as herein otherwise modified by this chapter bit is unlawful for any person to ride or drive within the municipal cemetery at a speed greater than ten 10 miles per hour caccess to roosevelt memorial park is restricted to daylight hours it is unlawful for any persons except the superintendent or his appointed representative to be in the cemetery after dark without prior written consent of the superintendent violation shall constitute a class c misdemeanor dno person shall use the cemetery ground or any roadway therein as a public thoroughfare or drive any vehicle grounds except for purposes of making deliveries in the cemetery or visiting any grave site ethe cemetery superintendent and his assistants shall have authority to direct all vehicular traffic and they are authorized to direct the parking or standing of all vehicles in said cemetery no person shall disobey or disregard the directions of the superintendent or his assistants relating to the movement or standing of all vehicles in said cemetery funless otherwise authorized by the superintendent or his assistants no person shall drive or move any vehicle within the cemetery except over a roadway open for vehicular traffic all roads not having an entrance and exit must be exited by the same way as entered including backing out of deadend roadways part  prior code  8230  children children under the age of eight years shall not be allowed in cemeteries unless accompanied by their parents or other adults except for the purposes of attending authorized funerals or in the company of adults placing flowers on the grave of a deceased relative or friend or performing any other customary evidence of respect in accordance with their religious principles   animals prohibited no animal shall be allowed in any cemetery except in the confines of a vehicle and must be at all times retained within the confines of said vehicle while the vehicle remains in the cemetery   decorum cemetery grounds are sacredly devoted to the interment and repose of the dead strict observance of decorum due such a place shall be required of all persons   injury to cemetery property prohibited ait is a class b misdemeanor for any person to tie or attempt to tie any horse animal or motor vehicle to any monument gravestone tablet marker tree shrub fence or enclosure on the premises of the cemetery for the purpose of injuring defacing or attempting the removal of same bit shall be an infraction for any person to injure deface break destroy or remove any headstone tombstone monument tree shrub or any other property in the cemetery   landscaping by private persons aexcept as provided by the rules and regulations of the governing body it is unlawful for any person to erect or maintain any fence corner post coping or boundary of any kind to plant any vegetation upon any lot or lots street alley or walk in the cemetery or to grade the ground or land thereof the cemetery superintendent shall whenever required furnish the true lines of any lots according to official survey shall prevent and prohibit any markings of the same except by official landmarks and shall prevent and prohibit any grading thereof that might destroy or interfere with the general slope of the land bthe excavation of lots or grave sites in the cemetery except as authorized by the cemetery superintendent is forbidden request for excavation or disinterment must be in writing and directed to the cemetery superintendent who may approve the same if the then current fee is paid and current rules regulations and cemetery policy are complied with including enhancement of the general appearance and functionality of the cemetery the city reserves the right to enter upon any grave to lay maintain and operate pipelines andor gutters for water supply or drainage the superintendent of the roosevelt city memorial park shall and does have the right to remove any shrub tree bush or other plant life andor obstruction to the irrigation sprinkling system in the cemetery excluding headstones andor monuments the superintendent also shallcan remove any object that is not in compliance with city regulations or that is disturbing the headstones he also maycanshall remove any object other than grave markers that is not beautifying to the cemeterys general appearance cthere shall be no person or persons maintaining any grounds in the cemetery except upon prior approval of the superintendent this includes but is not limited to mowing edging use of any kind of fertilizers pesticides or herbicides part  part  prior code  8235  placement of markers it is unlawful for any person to erect place or cause to be placed any marker or monument on any lot in cemetery in violation of the rules and regulations promulgated by the governing body regarding the placement construction and design of all such markers aall markers shall be made of granite or like material and shall be set in cement with a cement border of a minimum of six inches to a maximum of eight inches on both the front and the back of the marker there will be a border of not less than six inches in on either side of the marker the maximum outside border measurement of a single grave shall not exceed four feet in length from side to side the maximum outside border measurement of a double grave shall not exceed eight feet in length from side to side the maximum outside border measurement from front to back of monument cannot exceed thirty 30 inches in width no monument shall exceed the height of thirty 30 inches from the ground to the top of the monument all flower cup and vase inserts must be within the borders of the monument on either side and cannot be placed in either the front or back of the monument border twentyfour 24 hour notice must be given to the cemetery superintendent prior to placement of any marker thickness of cement base shall be no less than four inches bfootstones will be permitted with the same border size and only if they are set flush to the grass and are turned as to be read from the foot of the grave all footstones must be approved by the superintendent before installation and such installation must be done in his presence ca monument preparation fee will be set by resolution and adopted by the roosevelt city council dfamily stones monuments will be permitted if installed at the head of the grave or lot no family stone monument will be allowed at the foot or bottom of any lot or grave unless it meets the requirements of subsection b of this section part  part  prior code  8236  additional rules and regulations athe governing body may promulgate by resolution such additional rules and regulations concerning the care use operation and maintenance of the cemetery as it shall deem necessary bthe mayor may from time to time as the governing body deems necessary direct and publish a booklet of rules and regulations for the convenience of the purchasers of lots in the municipal cemetery such rules and regulations shall constitute a part of the terms and conditions under which owners and users may utilize the cemetery and shall form a supplement to this chapter after they have been adopted as official by resolution of the governing body cany changes in the rules and regulations shall be adopted by the governing body before such changes shall be official   collection of fees the recorderclerk and such other persons as the governing body may designate are authorized and required to collect in advance prices and fees for the opening and closing of graves or other services which shall include but not be limited to properly disinterring bodies and properly restoring the earth and grounds recording each burial disinterment or removal and raised monument privileges the fees shall be such amounts as are determined by the governing body from time to time by resolution   fee to be paid for opening grave ano grave shall be opened in the municipal cemetery until payment of a fee for the labor and expense in so opening the grave shall be paid bthe presentation of a receipt from the recorderclerk or person designated by the governing body when presented to the cemetery superintendent shall be authority to open a grave for the burial of a deceased person however upon a contract being entered into between any mortician and the municipality wherein the mortician agrees to be responsible and liable for fees for the opening of a grave and wherein that mortician will be personally liable for such fees and for perpetual care payments the recorderclerk or authorized person may give the cemetery superintendent authority to open graves without the presentation of a receipt from the recorderclerk or authorized person   purchase price and fees the governing body shall from time to time by resolution fix the size of lots the price at which burial rights shall be sold and the fees which shall be charged for the various cemetery services to be provided   sale of lots athe recorderclerk and such other person as the governing body may designate are authorized to sell the use of lots in the municipal cemetery for burial purposes only and to collect all sums arising from the sale the recorderclerk shall keep a complete record of all sales which record shall describe the location of the lot purchased and the price paid therefor the recorderclerk or designated person shall deliver to each purchaser a certificate of burial rights for each lot purchased which certificate shall among other things describe the location of the lot the purchase price and the type of maintenance services which are to be provided eg perpetual care prepaid continued maintenance or currently paid services ba certificate and rights to burial shall be exempt from execution taxation or assessment for care and maintenance from and after full payment of the purchase price payments made pursuant to this section shall not be construed to be in payment for cemetery services other than perpetual care or prepaid maintenance cperpetual care or prepaid continued maintenance shall be deemed to include the filling of the grave the placing of topsoil upon the grave seeding the grave with grass and watering and cutting the grass no other services are included dno other improvements changes or service except perpetual care or prepaid continued maintenance shall be made on any lot without the certificate holder or his heirs first submitting to and receiving from the cemetery superintendent written approval for such improvements changes or services which improvements changes or services shall be subject to the rules and regulations promulgated by the governing body ecemetery fees are based on residency as used herein the term resident shall mean and be defined as 1any person who was domiciled within the corporate limits of roosevelt utah at the time of death regardless of actual place of death  or 2any person owning real property within the corporate limits of roosevelt utah at the time of death regardless of the residence of domicile of such person  or 3any person who was a legal resident of roosevelt utah at the time of death regardless of domicile part  prior code  8251  restrictions of resale afrom and after  the lots sold by this municipality shall not be further sold transferred conveyed or assigned to any person except the municipality the municipality agrees to buy back any municipal cemetery grave lot which it may hereafter sell the repurchase of such lots shall be for the original price paid by the purchaser or the current selling price of the lot whichever is less bwhenever a certificate to burial rights or lots reverts to the municipality as provided for in this chapter or becomes vested in the municipality for any reason before new certificates are issued the original certificate shall be canceled or an assignment given and the record shall be so changed cthe certificates shall be issued and signed by the mayor and shall be attested by the recorderclerk all lots or parts of lots as provided in this section together with all improvements shall be exempt from execution and from taxation and assessment for care and maintenance charges from and after said payment dthis section shall not apply to sales or transfers to members of the immediate family but such sale or transfer shall not take effect until recorded in the office of the city recorder   descent and inheritance of burial rights upon death of the lot owner the lot descends to those named in hisher will or to hisher heirs as designated by law it is the descendants or heirs obligation to notify roosevelt city as to the change of ownership and the address of the new owner if the descendants do not notify the city they roosevelt city and the cemetery superintendent shall act upon their best judgment to determine heirs and successorships if in doing so in good faith the city makes an error neither the city nor the superintendent shall be liable for such error the heirs or successors are entitled to the same use and rights as the original owners and are bound by the same regulations providing that the lots andor graves have been paid for in full including perpetual care part prior code  8254  perpetual care acontracting for perpetual care 1no graves shall be opened on any new lot until perpetual care has been paid the remainder of the lot excluding the graves to be opened may be governed by contract wherein payment shall be agreed upon 2the agreement shall provide for a down payment in the amount of not less than twenty 20 percent of the total purchase price of the cost of the lot or portion thereof to be financed and shall further provide for the payment of monthly installments over a period of not more than twelve 12 months the monthly installments shall be in amounts equal to the balance of the contract divided by the total number of months which the contract is to run this includes a finance charge of ten 10 percent of the total cost of the lots andor graves less than twenty 20 percent down payment there will not be any penalty for prepayment of the contract nor will there be any reduction of interest charged if the contract is paid off early the interest is charged to offset the cost of bookkeeping and for the privilege of making payments on the lots andor graves 3the installment contract for perpetual care of or purchase of a lot with perpetual care shall provide for collection by the municipality in event of a default and such collection shall be by civil action and the defendant therein shall pay cost of collection together with a reasonable attorneys fee to the municipality and shall also pay interest at the rate of eight percent per annum upon the past due installments all installments shall immediately become due upon the default of any of the installments  provided however that when perpetual care for any lot in the municipal cemetery or portion thereof has not been paid for a period of ten 10 years then and in such an event the unused portion of the lot shall thereafter escheat to this municipality and the title thereof shall revert to this municipality which shall thereafter have the right option and privilege to sell and dispose of unused cemetery property as is in this chapter provided upon condition that this municipality shall thereafter maintain perpetually without cost of fee the portion of the lot occupied by a grave or graves prior to the date when the remaining property escheated to this municipality 4this municipality shall have power to fix by resolution a fee from any person now owning a cemetery lot or portion thereof for the annual maintenance and care thereof until such time as the fee shall be fixed by resolution said person shall pay a fee equal to zero dollars per year for such care and maintenance the fee shall continue to be paid until such time as a further or additional interment shall be made on the lot at which time the provisions of this section relating to perpetual care and maintenance and to payment of fees and costs pertaining thereto shall take effect and apply bcare included the essential perpetual care that the municipality agrees to give shall consist of care of the cemetery generally and shall include but is not limited to mowing of all lots and graves at reasonable intervals resodding seeding and filling in sunken graves sodding the surface of the graves to lot level removing dead flowers and trimming trees and shrubbery when necessary raking and cleaning the lots and straightening of tilting stones or markers but shall not include repairing or replacing markers or memorial structures of any nature except when the need for repair or replacement is directly caused by the municipality   part  prior code  8261 8262  burial of indigents athe governing body may by resolution designate a portion of the municipal cemetery to the burial of indigents whenever it is made to appear to the mayor by proof submitted to him by the recorderclerk that any person who has died does not have an estate sufficient to pay the purchase price of a lot in the cemetery and that the nearest relative or representative of such deceased person desires to have the body of such deceased interred in the cemetery the mayor may grant burial space for such deceased person at the request made to him by the recorderclerk bthe mayor shall communicate his decision to both the recorderclerk and the cemetery superintendent the mayor shall give report of his decision whether affirmative or negative to the governing body at its next regular meeting all strangers without funds or other persons who may die in the municipality may be granted the privilege granted herein   repossessions aall cemetery lots andor graves purchased before  without perpetual care and that same has not had perpetual care or yearly maintenance paid since  are in default the superintendent shall make a good faith reasonable attempt to provide actual notice to the owners or their heirs if actual notice has not been accomplished the superintendent shall cause notice to be published in the local newspaper for three consecutive weeks roosevelt city canwillshall repossess said lots andor graves if not contacted by letter or in person within a period of not less than sixty 60 days from date of last publication of notice to repossess or from date of actual notice 1the lot owners canshall pay all back maintenance fees plus interest the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council for a single grave and for a full lot seven to eight graves and they will also pay the current fee for conversion from yearly maintenance to perpetual care 2any occupied graves are exempt from the repossession as set forth above and will be cared for as if perpetual care was paid in full after the remainder of the lot is repossessed 3all lots andor graves purchased after  are subject to the same regulations after a period of not less than fifteen 15 years from date of purchase 4any lots andor graves found in default by the above means will be deemed abandoned and shall be resold by the city as it deems appropriate ball lots andor graves purchased with perpetual care or that have been converted to perpetual care that have more than five grave spaces with two or less occupied will be deemed abandoned if no new burial is conducted within a fifty 50 year period from date of purchase or date of last burial all lots andor graves mentioned above that are deemed abandoned will be repossessed by roosevelt city after the fifty 50 year period is over and sold on a firstcome basis 1no remains of any person occupying any grave space will be disinterred as to cause reason for the lot to be deemed abandoned cif the lot or grave owners or their heirs intend to retain burial rights they may retain their rights from repossession by submitting in writing a document stating such intentions 1this document must be accompanied by a recording fee the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council 2all intent to hold documents must be filed every thirty 30 years or said lots andor graves will be repossessed in accordance with the repossession provisions of this code part  part  decoration of graves aall decorations must be placed and maintained within the cement border of the monument placement of benches is not responsible for inadvertent scratches and chips that occur from routine maintenance such happenings are a risk assumed by the owners of the monuments and are a condition that goes with the operation and maintenance of the water system of the municipality bsuperintendent there is created the position of superintendent of the water department cduties of the superintendent the superintendent of the water system shall manage and supervise the municipal water system pursuant to the provisions of this article and pursuant to resolutions rules and regulations adopted by the governing body from time to time prescribing his powers and duties and directing the manner and frequency with which he shall make reports to the mayor relating to the water system all of the functions and activities of the superintendent shall be carried on under the direction of the mayor   application for water use procedure aincity all applications for the use of water must be made on forms furnished by the city and signed by the applicant the applicant shall state fully and truthfully the purpose for which water is required and shall agree to and be covered by such rules and regulations as may be prescribed by the city for the control of the water supply the applicant shall agree to be responsible for and agree to pay all bills due the city on account of materials andor labor furnished as well as all water supplied to the premises before water will be turned over to any premises all charges against the premises that are due and payable to the city for water sewer and garbage or any services materials or supplies pertaining thereto furnished thereon must be paid in full boutofcity in addition to complying with the aforementioned incity procedure an outofcity applicant must personally appear before the city council at a regularly scheduled city council meeting to make a formal request for service and to answer any questions the council may have the council must by motion give the outofcity applicant permission to proceed with the applications a a  water deposit requireduse thereof at the time any applicant shall apply for utility service with the city a refundable security deposit the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council shall be required if the account is held in the name of the person who owns the property for which the service will be used the deposit is refundable after one full year twelve 12 consecutive months of timely payments otherwise the deposit will be held until the account is closed whenever a utility customer shall have failed to pay for water sewer or garbage service supplied or services rendered to such premises the money deposited or any part thereof may be applied to the payment of such delinquent closed account by the treasurer the deposit is required at the time service begins whenever water consumers are not the actual owners but merely buying under contract or bond or deed or in work of extending the water connection from the point to which the municipality installs it to the place at which the water is to be used shall be my responsibility and shall be performed at my sole cost b the connection so made by the municipality including the meter shall remain the property of the municipality at all times and the municipality shall have access thereto at all times 2the location of the meter whether on my premises or at some point near my premises may be decided solely by the municipality 3before making connection with the water system i shall cause the plumbing upon my premises to be inspected by the municipality and if the plumbing is not approved i will cause the plumbing to be rectified at my own expense to meet the requirements of the municipality or of any other governmental agency having jurisdic tion to regulate the water system within the municipality 4i will be bound by the rules regulations resolutions or ordinances enacted now or hereafter by the over the eight thousand 8000 gallons all such rates shall be uniformly assessed and reflect the increased costs of water service 2all water rates for service outside the city shall be one and onehalf times the incity rate part   res 2000183    special rates the governing body may from time to time fix by agreement or resolution special rates and conditions for users using exceptionally large thousand 1000 gallons this price shall remain in effect until such time as it is deemed necessary to adjust the rate according to the 1986 agreement see copy of 1986 neola water agreement attached to the ordinance codified in this section bballard town sewage treatment wholesale rate roosevelt city shall accept and treat the effluent discharged from homes and businesses in the town of ballard pursuant to the 1986 agreement this agreement establishes the rates for treatment based on two separate and distinct categories the first category is for all businesses and residences which impact the independence road line the second category being all other effluent which does not impact the independence road line 1the current cost to ballard town for roosevelt city to treat the effluent that impacts the independence road line shall be as follows acommercial the amount set by resolution of the city council per first five thousand 5000 gallons of water used per month and the amount set by resolution of the city council per each additional one thousand 1000 gallons of water used per month bresidential the amount set by resolution of the city council 2the cost to ballard town for roosevelt city to treat their effluent that does not impact the independence road line will be set by resolution of the city council per each thousand 1000 gallons of effluent that enters the lagoon facility these prices shall remain in effect until such time as it is deemed necessary to adjust the rates pursuant to the 1986 agreement see copy of 1986 ballard sewer agreement attached to the ordinance codified in this section part     board of equalization rates and rebates the governing body is constituted a board of equalization of water rates to hear complaints and make corrections of any assessments deemed to be illegal unequal or unjust they may if they see fit rebate all or any part of the water bill of any indigent person   use without payment prohibited it is unlawful for any person by himself family servants or agents to utilize the municipal water or sewer system without paying therefor as herein provided or without authority to open any fire hydrant stopcock valve or other fixtures attached to the system of water supply unless it is done pursuant to proper application agreement or resolution it is unlawful to injure deface or impair any part or appurtenance of the water or sewer system or to cast anything into any reservoir or tank belonging to the water system   delinquencydiscontinuance of service athe recorderclerk or water supervisor shall furnish to each user or mail to or leave at his place of residence or usual place of business a written or printed statement stating thereon the amount of water service charges assessed against him once each month or at such other regular interval as the governing body shall direct bthe statement shall specify the amount of the bill for the water service and the place of payment and date due if any person fails to pay the water charges within thirty 30 days of the date due the recorderclerk or water supervisor shall give the customer notice in writing of intent to discontinue the service to the customer unless the customer pays the bill in full within five days from the date of notice cif the water service is thereafter discontinued for failure to make payment then before the water service to the premises shall again be provided all delinquent water charges must have been paid to the treasurer or arrangements made for their payment in a manner satisfactory to the municipality in the event water is turned off for nonpayment of water charges then before the water service to the premises shall again be provided the customer shall pay in addition to all delinquent water charges such extra charge for turning the water on and off the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council furthermore in addition to such payments and penalties a delinquent customer may be required to make and file a new application and deposit if the previous deposit has theretofore been applied to the payment of delinquent bills the recorderclerk is authorized and empowered to enforce the payment of all delinquent water charges by an action at law in the name of the municipality part  prior code  14121  water deposit required after shutoff due to delinquent bill on a utility account if water is shut off due to the nonpayment of a delinquent bill and if a deposit is not on the account then a deposit the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council will be required to turn the water back on after the delinquent bill is paid in full if there is a deposit on the account then the delinquent bill must be paid in full before water can be turned on no water deposit will be refunded until one full year of no delinquencies is achieved a service charge the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council shall be assessed to turn the water on the first time each and every time thereafter it shall be a service charge the amount of which will be set by resolution of the city council part  c c  responsibility of owner for charges it shall be unlawful for a tenant or the owner of any property to connect into the water system without first making application for services from roosevelt city said written application shall contain an agreement signed by the owner or his duly authorized agent to the effect that in consideration of granting such application the owner will pay for all services furnished such tenant or any other occupant of the premises named in the application in case such tenant or occupant shall fail to pay for the same according to the ordinances of the city d d  owner or subscribers responsibility to maintain accessibility to meters by city employees it shall be the property owners or the resident utility subscribers responsibility to provide an unencumbered access to the water meter for purposes of monthly reading to determine the amount of water used in the event that a property owner or resident subscriber blocks the access by any means whatsoever either intentional or unintentional the city shall deliver one written warning to the property owner or subscriber to remove the obstacle so that the meters may be easily accessed if after the written warning the owner or subscriber does not comply by removing the obstacle barrier or obstruction including dogs within two weeks of receipt of the warning the city shall bill the owner or resident twice the typical monthly rate until such obstruction barrier or obstacle is removed at no time will any portion of the double rate be refunded or applied to the account even if it is determined that less water was actually used e e  penalty for turning water into residence or using utility services without proper application and permission to activate water service without proper application and permission from the city shall constitute a theft of services pursuant to utah shall be punishable as a misdemeanor or felony depending upon the amount involved to use an existing connection to supply water to a residence dwelling trailer or any other structure not attached to or considered a part of the structure for which a connection has been obtained also constitutes a theft of services and shall be punishable as a misdemeanor or felony depending upon the amount and shall result in the loss of water service to the structure from which the water is being used also if a water subscriber is guilty of this he shall be required to pay a one hundred dollar $10000 penalty before applying for water under the provisions of this article f f  delinquent payment defined and shutoff timetable establishedpenalty assigned a bill for water service becomes delinquent if not paid by the twentyfifth day of the month the billing went out at that time a ten 10 percent penalty shall be attached if the delinquent amount plus penalty are not paid in full by the time the next billing goes out a notice will be attached stating that all charges current and delinquent must be paid by the twentieth of the current month or the water will be shut off once the water is shut off the procedure to reinstate service shall be as ordained herewith g g  turning on water after being turned off prohibited it is unlawful for any person after the water has been turned off from the premises for nonpayment of water charges or other violation of the ordinances rules regulations or resolutions pertaining to the water supply to turn on or allow the water to be turned on or used without authority from the superintendent or recorderclerk   separate connections it is unlawful for two or more families or service users to be supplied from the same service pipe connection or water meter unless special permission for such combination usage has been granted by the governing body and the premises served are owned by the same owner in all such cases a failure on the part of any one of the users to comply with this section shall warrant a withholding of a supply of water service connections until compliance or payment has been made and in any event the property owner shall be primarily liable to the municipality for all water services utilized on all such premises nothing herein shall be deemed to preclude the power of the municipality to require separate pipes connections or meters at a subsequent time   unauthorized users it is unlawful for any water service user to permit any person from other premises or any unauthorized person to use or obtain water services regularly from his premises or water facilities either outside or inside his premises   period for visitors individuals visiting the premises of an authorized user in a recreational vehicle not including a mobilehome and continuing to live therein during the period of visitation may receive water service from the service pipes or facilities of the host during the visitation period which shall not exceed thirty 30 days continued use thereafter shall be deemed unauthorized and violative of the provisions of this part relating to separate connections and unauthorized use   pipes to be kept in good repair all users of water services shall keep their service pipes and connections and other apparatus in good repair and protected from frost at their own expense no person except under the direction of the water superintendent shall be allowed to dig into the street for the purpose of laying removing or repairing any service pipe   quality of service pipe aall service and other pipe used in conjunction with the water services of the municipality shall be of such material quality and specifications as the governing body may from time to time by resolution provide and shall be installed at such distances below ground as may be specified by regulations relating to the water department all work alterations or extensions affecting water pipes shall be subject to the acceptance of the water superintendent and no connections with any water mains shall be made without first obtaining a permit therefor from the recorderclerk bno consumer shall be permitted to conduct water pipes across lots or buildings to adjoining premises without permission from the water superintendent and subject to such requirements relating to controls as may be imposed by him   faulty equipment it is unlawful for any water user to awaste water  ballow it to be wasted by stops taps valves leaky joints or pipes or to allow tanks or watering troughs to leak or overflow  cwastefully run water from hydrants faucets or stops or water closets urinals sinks or other apparatus  duse the water for purposes other than for those which he has applied or to use water in violation of the rules and regulations for controlling the water supply   sprinkling vehicles vehicles for sprinkling shall be regulated and controlled by the water department superintendent of the water department   department to have free access the water superintendent and his agents shall at all ordinary hours have free access to any place supplied with water services from the municipal system for the purpose of examining the apparatus and ascertaining the amount of water service being used and the manner of its use   nonliability for damages the municipality shall not be liable for any damage to a water service user by reason of stoppage or interruption of his or her water supply service caused by fires scarcity of water accidents to the water system or its mains or which occurs as the result of maintenance and extension operations or from any other unavoidable cause this section shall not be construed to extend the liability of the municipality beyond that provided in the governmental immunity act   water not supplied for motors syphons etc no water shall be supplied from the pipes of the municipal water system for the purpose of driving motor syphon turbine or other wheels or any hydraulic engines or elevators or for driving or propelling machinery of any kind whatsoever nor shall any license be granted or issued for any such purpose except by special permission of the governing body   sprinklers ait is unlawful for any person to use such number of outlets simultaneously or to use such sprinkler or combinations of sprinkler or outlets as will in the opinion of the governing body materially affect the pressure or supply of water in the municipal water system or any part thereof and the governing body may from time to time by resolution specify combinations or numbers of outlets which may have such effect bthe governing body shall after determining that such improper use exists notify the affected water user or the owner of the premises whereon such use occurs of such determination in writing order such use discontinued and advise that such continued usage constitutes a violation of this chapter   scarcity of water in time of scarcity of water whenever it shall in the judgment of the mayor and the governing body be necessary the mayor shall by proclamation limit the use of water to such extent as may be necessary it is unlawful for any person his family servants or agents to violate any proclamation made by the mayor in pursuance of this part   outsidecity service any water service that is outside the corporate boundaries of the city is established as a benefit from the city at no time is outside city utility service including water considered an obligation except upon special written agreement as approved by the city council in the event that a water shortage is experienced the city may at its option discontinue service to all outside connections except those resulting from rightsofway currently being used to transmit water from the source into the city    waste of water ausers of water from the municipal water system shall not permit water to continue to run wastefully and without due efforts to conserve water if in the judgment of the water superintendent or of any of the officers of the municipality a user of municipal water engages in practices which result in the needless waste of water and continues so to do after reasonable notice to discontinue wastefulness has been given the superintendent or any officer may refer the matter to the governing body bthe governing body may thereupon consider terminating the right of the individual to use culinary water if it elects to consider the matter of termination it shall give notice to the water user of the intention to terminate his water connection at least five days prior to the meeting of the governing body at which termination of water service is to be considered the notice shall inform him of the time and place of the meeting and of the charges which lead to the consideration of the termination ca water user whose right to utilize municipal water is being reviewed shall have opportunity to appear with or without counsel and present his reasons why his water service should not be discontinued dafter due hearing the governing body may arrive at a determination if the determination is to discontinue the wasteful water users service connection it shall notify him of the decision and of the period during which the service will remain discontinued   metering ameter installationsfailure to register all water subscribed to malfunctions and fails to register the water shall be charged for the time the meter is out of order at the average daily rate as registered by the meter for the previous meter reading period when the meter was in order bmeterinjuring removing it shall be unlawful for any person by himself family employee or agents to open interfere with injure deface or in anywise impair the workings of any meter from the premises to do so can result in the loss of water service to the premises andor the city can cause the person who removes or tampers or causes to remove or tamper with to be cited for such which constitutes a class b misdemeanor cmaintenance of service connection the city will maintain all water connections from the point of connection with the water main up to and including the meter responsibility shall end at the master meter the number size and location of all master meters shall be determined by the city where individual meters exist instead of master meters the city shall aapplications for permits to make water connections or other alteration or for laying or repairing lines connected directly or indirectly to the municipal water system must be made in writing by a licensed plumber his authorized agent or by the owner of the premises who shall describe the nature of the work to be done for which the application is made the application shall be granted if the superintendent determines that 1the connection repair alteration or installation will cause no damage to the street in which the water main is laid or that it will not be prejudicial to the interests of persons whose property has been or may thereafter be connected to the water main 2the connection conforms to the ordinances regulations specifications and standards of materials required by the municipality all connections alterations or installations shall be to the line and grade designated by the water superintendent bfees for permits or for inspection services shall be of such amounts as the governing body shall from time to time determine by resolution   moving or replacement of water lines in the event that the municipality in its sole discretion determines that any water line of of reconnecting such new line or lines from the house of the customer to his property line shall be borne by the customer   when permits shall not be issued permission to connect with the municipal water system shall not be given unless the plumbing in the house or building to be connected meets the provisions of the building and plumbing codes of the municipality   discontinuance of service any customer desiring to discontinue service shall notify the municipality in writing of such fact at least ten 10 days before the date when such service shall be discontinued on giving such written notice the customer shall not be responsible for water bills incurred after the date specified in the notice any credit balance in favor of the customer as a result of an advance payment of bills or a deposit made will be refunded upon discontinuance of service   fire hydrants water for fire hydrants will be furnished free of charge by the municipality installation and repairs on such hydrants maintain such hydrants on their premises if the municipality concludes that hydrants shall be so installed for the protection of the residents of the municipality   extension of water mains within the accompanied by a map showing the location of the proposed extension together with an offer to advance the whole expense thereof which cost shall be verified by the water superintendent the governing body may grant or deny the petition as in its discretion seems best for the welfare of existing water users in the municipality bcost of extensions determined upon the receipt of such petition and map the applicant 2in the event any deposit remains unclaimed for a period of five years after the depositor has discontinued water service the deposit may be forfeited and then transferred to the water materials and labor   water conservation plan1 this chapter is hereby amended to include the roosevelt city water conservation plan and will be reviewed and amended as needed no less than every five years the water conservation plan will continue to play a vital role in the future development of roosevelt city  secondary water service  required connection be it hereby ordained by the roosevelt city council that all residential lots and all business lots that water outside shall hook onto the secondary system within ninety 90 days of delivery of water to the lots by the city furthermore there is no provision for exemption from this requirement however in the case of extreme hardship as determined by a majority vote of the city council the connection fee can be made in twelve 12 equal installments provided they are made each month for twelve 12 consecutive months fees will be established by resolution and may change from year to year   culinary system must be completely separate from the secondary system once the secondary water is delivered to a lot the property owner must sever any connection configuration that could possibly cause a crossconnection with the culinary water and the secondary water failure to do this could cause contamination into the culinary system should this occur the property owner is the responsible party   sprinkling required due to pressure constraints and best use of secondary water roosevelt city deems it necessary that all secondary water shall be used approved sprinkling system no flood irrigation will be allowed   connection fees and monthly service fees all residential lots and all business or commercial lots that water outside must pay the appropriate connection fee within ninety 90 days of being billed the connection fee shall be set by resolution all residential lot owners are responsible to pay the monthly service fee based upon the rate schedule set by resolution failure to pay the monthly service fee for the secondary water within the same time limit requirement for culinary water shall result in penalties and interest in a like manner as the culinary water both culinary and secondary water service can be terminated to any residential lot and commercial lot for nonpayment according to ordinance and policy as constituted by the city of roosevelt 1 s note the roosevelt city water conservation plan can be viable generally  purposeencouragement of irrigation systems the city encourages the development of pressurized irrigation systems within the city whenever feasible to conserve on culinary water costs and culinary system capacity   determination of feasibility the city will install a pressurized irrigation system when feasible as determined by the number of users availability of water cost of construction and other relevant factors 1  applicationconnection fees aall users of said system must complete an application for irrigation water and pay the connection fees as established by the city council if the connection is approved the city shall install the necessary piping and valves to complete the connection to the nearest property line if the connection is not approved the connection fee will be refunded bwater shares may be turned in to the city in exchange for connection fees cthe water can only be used on the property that has paid the connection fee 2 6 8  annual fee all users of each pressurized irrigation system shall pay an annual fee before they can use water from the system the city shall estimate the cost of operations and replacements each spring and send out a billing of this amount connections will be turned on only if the annual fee has been paid in full 3  easements for neighbors each user shall be required to provide the necessary easements for neighbors to utilize the system as a condition of connection approval 4  damage to private sprinkling systems the city shall not be liable for any damages resulting from the use of said system to private sprinkling systems 5  crossconnections to culinary system prohibited crossconnections between the culinary system and the irrigation systems are prohibited 7  termination of service the city may terminate water services if the provisions of are not met by the user 9  irrigation ditch defined an irrigation ditch means any ditch or canal irrigation water is controlled or distributed  part prior code  10510  headgate required it is unlawful for any person to convey water from an irrigation ditch to his lot or premises by an irrigation ditch without having first constructed a substantial headgate at the point of diversion such headgate shall be kept closed and watertight except during the period allotted to him for the use of such water where any irrigation ditch crosses any portion of a sidewalk such ditch shall be contained in pipe or other substantial material the covering of which shall be on a level with such sidewalk  part prior code  10520  careful construction of ditches required the conveyance of irrigation water shall be done with the least possible injury to property both in constructing the necessary ditches and managing the water flow therein persons taking delivery of water from such ditches shall be liable for all damages caused by negligence in the construction of said ditches or in the management of water flowing therein  part prior code  10530  disposition of wastewater it shall be the duty of all persons using water for irrigation or other purposes to conduct the surplus water or wastewater into an irrigation ditch and it shall be unlawful for any person to permit such water to flood streets sidewalks or private property to the damage thereof or to run to unnecessary waste  part prior code  10540  penalty any person found guilty of violating any portion of shall be guilty of a class b misdemeanor  part prior code  10550 water service in exchange for irrigation water shares  policy it is the policy of roosevelt city to service customers both outside and inside its corporate boundaries with culinary water so far as an adequate supply is available and the service is subordinate to the roosevelt city residents aroosevelt city residents are defined as any service subscribed to that will be metered and delivered inside the city limits boutofcity service is defined as any service metered and delivered outside the corporate boundaries of the city   surrender of shares required whenever possible and at all times when a request is made for culinary water service and the property has a source of irrigation water on it shares must be surrendered to roosevelt city for this service   application for service any land agent developer real estate subdivider individual partnership company or corporation desiring to be serviced by the roosevelt city culinary water system must make application for such service before the elected officials of the city in order to receive this service valid stock in a water irrigation company must be surrendered to the city to help offset impact and connection fees whenever possible   criteria for approval when a request is made for culinary water service outside the city limits the following criteria shall be met afor every acre or part of an acre of land to be serviced or for each connection requested to be serviced by the roosevelt culinary water system one share of usable irrigation stock in an active and viable irrigation company shall be tendered to roosevelt city bthe price of each water connection serviced shall be reduced by a dollar amount per share of irrigation stock as agreed to by the party requesting service and the majority of the elected body of the governing officials of roosevelt city cthe cost of incity water service can also be exchanged for stock in a usable and viable irrigation company upon agreement with the party requesting service and a majority of the elected body of the governing officials of roosevelt city   requirements for incity service the exchange of irrigation water stock is offered as an option to the subscribing entity for outofcity service exchange of irrigation water stock is mandatory as described in the governing body of the city may allow a subscriber to purchase an outofcity connection without exchanging irrigation stock if it is the opinion and upon a majority vote of the city council that the exchange requirement is not practical or would place an undue hardship on the subscriber   water must be viable irrigation water stock that is exchanged for culinary water service must be viable and usable to wastes of unusual characteristics or making use thereof under exceptional circumstances   board of equalization rates and rebates the governing body is constituted a board of equalization of sewer rates to hear complaints and make corrections of any assessments or charges deemed to be illegal unequal or unjust   delinquencyright to hearingdiscontinuance of service if any person entity or business fails to pay for sewer charges within thirty 30 days of the due date the treasurerclerk or other designated city employee shall give the customer notice in writing of the intent to discontinue the service of water to the premises unless the customer pays the bill in full within ten 10 days from the date of notice said written notice shall state that the customer has the right to request a hearing on the matter before the governing body city council within the ten 10 day period if the hearing is requested service of water shall not be discontinued pending the outcome of the hearing if no hearing is requested the right to hearing shall be deemed waived and the city may proceed to obtain discontinuance of water service as well as pursue any other remedies available in the event city water is not being used the sewer may be disconnected from the premises upon notice and hearing or waiver thereof pursuant to the procedures set forth in this section    prior code  14219  definitions unless the context specifically indicates otherwise the meaning of terms used in this chapter shall be as follows bod denoting biochemical oxygen demand means the quantity of oxygen utilized in the biochemical oxidation of organic matter under standard laboratory procedure in five days at twenty 20 degrees celsius expressed in milligrams per liter building drain means that part of the lowest horizontal piping of a drainage system which receives the discharge from soil waste and other drainage pipes inside the walls of the building and conveys it to the building sewer beginning five feet 15 meters outside the inner face of the building wall building inspector means the building inspector of the city of roosevelt or his authorized deputy agent or representative building sewer means the extension from the building drain to the public sewer or other place of disposal combined sewer means a sewer receiving both surface runoff and sewage garbage means solid wastes from the domestic and commercial preparation cooking and dispensing of food and from the handling storage and sale of produce industrial wastes means the liquid wastes from industrial manufacturing processes trade or business as distinct from sanitary sewage natural outlet means any outlet into a watercourse pond ditch lake or other body of surface or groundwater person means any individual firm company association society corporation or group ph means the logarithm of the reciprocal of the weight of hydrogen ions in grams per liter of solution properly shredded garbage means the wastes from the preparation cooking and dispensing of food that have been shredded to such a degree that all particles will be carried freely under the flow conditions normally prevailing in public sewers with no particle greater than onehalf inch 127 centimeters in any dimension public sewer means a sewer in which all owners of abutting properties have equal rights and is controlled by public authority sanitary sewer means a sewer which carries sewage and to which storm surface and groundwaters are not intentionally admitted sewage means a combination of the watercarried wastes from residences business buildings institutions and industrial establishments together with such ground surface and stormwaters as may be present sewage treatment plant means any arrangement of devices and structures used for treating sewage sewage works means all facilities for collecting pumping treating and disposing of sewage sewer means a pipe or conduit for carrying sewage shall is mandatory  may is permissive slug means any discharge of water sewage or industrial waste which in concentration of any given constituent or in quantity of flow exceeds for any period of duration longer than fifteen 15 minutes more than five times the average twentyfour 24 hour concentration or flows during normal operation storm drain sometimes termed storm sewer means a sewer which carries storm and surface waters and drainage but excludes sewage and industrial wastes other than unpolluted cooling water suspended solids means solids that either float on the surface of or are in suspension in water sewage or other liquids and which are removable by laboratory filtering watercourse means a channel in which a flow of water occurs either continuously or intermittently   use of public sewers required ait works and to determine the existence of hazard to life limb and property the particular analyses involved will determine whether a twentyfour 24 hour composite of all outfalls of a premises is appropriate or whether a grab sample or samples should be taken normally but not always bod and suspended solids analyses are obtained from twentyfour 24 hour composites of all outfalls whereas phs
